function autoScroll() {
  var scroll = document.createElement('div');
  document.body.appendChild(scroll);
  document.addEventListener("scroll", function(event) {
    if (event.stopPropagation()) {
      if (!document.getElementById('auto-scroll')) {
        document.getElementById('auto-scroll').style.left = '0px';
        document.getElementById('auto-scroll').style.top = '0px';
        document.getElementById('auto-scroll').style.width = '100%';
        document.getElementById('auto-scroll').style.height = '100%';
      }
  });
}
